<h1
  className={"openapi__heading"}
>
  app.bsky.feed.getPosts
</h1>

<MethodEndpoint
  method={"get"}
  path={"app.bsky.feed.getPosts"}
>
  
</MethodEndpoint>



Gets post views for a specified list of posts (by AT-URI). This is sometimes referred to as 'hydrating' a 'feed skeleton'.
